<review>JAB owns & has to manage a lot of properties. It would help, if they had a stronger & more honest workforce. The office has 3-4 ladies. It seems like one lady does the applications, one lady sees to parking issues, & the other lady is the manager. So you would think the various duties would be handled equally and properly in a timely manner with good results. That does not happen at all.
On the other hand, they have only 2 honest, dedicated, diligent & knowledgeable maintenance workers.

The office staff has changed management quite a few times within the last 6 years.  Their 'customer service' over the phone & in person is terrible because to manage is not everyone's cup of tea.
One can feel a lot of discrimination in their attitude when dealing with residents.
One person has to pay the application fee to be added on to the lease. Another person has his family members staying with him for years without being on the lease.
One person has to pay the pet deposit. The other person has a cat & dog, etc., & hides it from the JAB office.

Only a few tenants are given new rules by JAB about 'allowed parking'. My neighbor was told 'illegally parked' so he moved his car. I wonder on what basis was he discriminated ? because other tenants & guests leave their cars in the guest spots for a very long period of time without moving it (just like he did), but only he was given the illegal parking notice. It goes to say that JAB has very poor guidelines that they follow or they just don't care, or they underestimate their tenants, hoping one wouldn't notice their unprofessionalism.
On JAB's application, there is a question that asks whether you make 3 times the rent? I have 'ghetto' type neighbors who don't work, smoke weed a lot, argue/ fight quite often, have a cat & dog.. & JAB doesn't do anything about it.
One should read Darlene's profile [manager] on the JAB website. There are sweet complimentary words about her to make her appear such a lovely person. She tries her best to avoid talking to you because you are making a valid point. She makes you feel so unwelcome, & encourages you to move out. Her co-worker has told me that Darlene has issues so it is best to avoid her. The office ladies are greedy, & want to maintain their positions. They really do nothing to make you feel at home nor do they help the community of Stockton.

The JAB office is far away from a lot of their properties so residents/ guests do things outside of their lease agreement because they know that JAB is not watching.

The JAB staff do not do a good job in maintaining their properties. They do the bare minimum. They do not seem to care, as long as they get their money on time.
The office staff do not like receiving work orders nor are they helpful towards the concerns tenants may have.< /review>< Pictures>

<review>As for member service over the phone, it really depends on which representative you get connected with. Some are impatient, but there are some that are professional and nice enough.

However, I am really upset by how some of the LA Care service representatives handle NON-English speaker calls. Although these individuals do not speak English, they are regardless your members who have every right to receive the services that their plan provides and for which they are enrolled.

Since LA Care requires that each member call in personally for privacy purposes, these non-English speakers must call in on their own and do their best to request translation services, which I am grateful that LA Care provides. However, I have had multiple, non-English-speaking relatives and acquaintances tell me that they had service representatives HANG UP on their calls while they were trying to do their best to read off their member ID or even before they got a chance to request a translator because the representatives could tell from their stuttering/accent that this was going to be a troublesome call.

While I understand that non-English speaker calls take more time and effort, shoving them aside for your convenience is still no way to treat these members. PLEASE at least make the effort to kindly ask them if they would like a translator. These members are aware of their own handicap, so they are familiar with the term ‚Äútranslator/translation,‚Äù and they will be grateful.

The place was recommended to me so i took some clients, and after a very long day it was the perfect tonic.

Ohhh how vinegar and fermented things have become ‚Äòthe‚Äô trend... but this place actually leans into this trend very well. the interior is very nice but not overly stuffy. the one detracting point here is that the communal tables for seating are surrounded with benches which discourages you from hanging out after eating all your slices of za.

< Text>
I purchased my mattress from Mattress Firm a little over a year ago (original review below) and I wanted to upgrade my pillows. I initial bought some cheap pillows off of Amazon when I purchased my bed and now a year later and the pillows are lumpy and causing me some discomfort in my neck. I decided it was time to invest in some good quality pillows, so I reached out to Mesfin who was still with the company (thank God!) and he advised me that I should come into the store during their Memorial Day Sale to test out some options.

Mesfin educated me on the importance of a good pillow. He had me test out several pillows, on the exact make and model of the bed that I initial purchased from Mattress Firm, so that I could see how the pillow felt on top of my actual bed! Who would have thought that, that was a thing?!! Makes sense though when you think about it.

I purchased 2 great pillows. I'm so glad that I did not purchase the pillows online and that I took the time to come into the store. I am even more thankful that Mesfin helped me with something so trival as picking out pillows.

Once again, I've had a great experience with Mattress Firm & Mesfin. I will be going back for all my future mattress and of course pillow needs!

Review as of 2/22/18

As a woman I am always leery of being taken advantage of when it comes to things such as getting any work done on my vehicle, or in this case buying a brand-new mattress.  I went to Mattress Firm to do some preliminary research before I made a purchase. I was greeted by the store manager, Mesfin, who was welcoming and personable. He took me around the show room and educated me on each mattress. He was extremely knowledgeable about their selection of mattresses and was very patient with me. I tested each one out and by process of elimination, he helped me find the perfect mattress for me. He took his time and answered all my questions, he really exceeded all my expectations. When I was finally ready to make my purchase 2 weeks later, he even helped me get financing!  Overall, I had a pleasant experience, Mesfin took the nervousness and anxiety out of making such a huge purchase.<//Text>

< Text>
My wife and I love to go to the different bowling alleys in the towns we visit. This place is dated but in an awesome way. I was shot back into the late 70's. There are 16 lanes some are upper and some are on a lower floor. The staff are very nice.  They have a small snack bar with typical bowling alley prices. We didn't eat here but saw some food and it looked good. The lanes were a bit difficult to bowl on but that's why we like visiting other lanes to see differences from ours back home.< /Text>

I have been a customer for 25 years.  Since this visit dealt with the need for a new FOB key for a car- the staff try to bully you to purchase from their expensive supplier.  I have found another locksmith that is half their price.

I went back after four months since I left my review above.
I needed a "laser" cut key.   Note: No laser involved- it is just a milling unit that cuts in the middle of the key instead of the edge.
The cost for "Key Evidence" to cut?  $50.00.  Mine was a one edge key.  The Rep looked at my blank.  (My own blank)
I declined service and went to Ace Hardware just a minute up the road. I paid $10.00.  Key works great.

Key evidence is now the place of last resort for me.

I have since learned to program my own keys via computer -  all motivated by being treated with contempt just for wanting to get a spare key for a modern 5 year old car.   I saved over $200.00 by purchasing online from a good source and paying Ace hardware to cut the blank.   The programming cable cost $20.00.< /Text>
